I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Security] NVIDIA API key exposed in process list when creating inference provider
During onboarding, `openshell provider create` is called with the API key interpolated directly into the shell command:

```
openshell provider create --name nvidia-nim --type openai \
  --credential "NVIDIA_API_KEY=${process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY}" ...
```

While this command is running, any user on the machine can see the full API key via `ps aux`. On shared systems (e.g., DGX Spark), this is a real credential exposure risk.

**Expected:** Pass the credential via stdin, environment variable, or a temporary file with restricted permissions — not as a command-line argument.

Related PRs that partially address this:
- #148 — replace shell string interpolation with argv arrays
- #191 — use provider-specific credential environment variable

</pr_description>

Can you help me implement the necessary changes to the repository so that the requirements specified in the <pr_description> are met?

    67	/**
    68	 * Check if a sandbox is in Ready state from `openshell sandbox list` output.
    69	 * Strips ANSI codes and exact-matches the sandbox name in the first column.
    70	 */
    71	function isSandboxReady(output, sandboxName) {
    72	  const clean = output.replace(/\x1b\[[0-9;]*m/g, "");
    73	  return clean.split("\n").some((l) => {
    74	    const cols = l.trim().split(/\s+/);
    75	    return cols[0] === sandboxName && cols.includes("Ready") && !cols.includes("NotReady");
    76	  });
    77	}

    82	 * @param {string} gwInfoOutput - Raw output from `openshell gateway info -g nemoclaw`.

    85	function hasStaleGateway(gwInfoOutput) {

    89	function streamSandboxCreate(command) {
    90	  const child = spawn("bash", ["-lc", command], {
    91	    cwd: ROOT,
    92	    env: process.env,
    93	    stdio: ["ignore", "pipe", "pipe"],
    94	  });
    95	
    96	  const lines = [];
    97	  let pending = "";
    98	  let lastPrintedLine = "";
    99	  let sawProgress = false;
   100	  let settled = false;
   101	
   102	  function shouldShowLine(line) {
   103	    return (
   104	      /^  Building image /.test(line) ||
   105	      /^  Context: /.test(line) ||
   106	      /^  Gateway: /.test(line) ||
   107	      /^Successfully built /.test(line) ||
   108	      /^Successfully tagged /.test(line) ||
   109	      /^  Built image /.test(line) ||
   110	      /^  Pushing image /.test(line) ||
   111	      /^\s*\[progress\]/.test(line) ||
   112	      /^  Image .*available in the gateway/.test(line) ||
   113	      /^Created sandbox: /.test(line) ||
   114	      /^✓ /.test(line)
   115	    );
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  function flushLine(rawLine) {
   119	    const line = rawLine.replace(/\r/g, "").trimEnd();
   120	    if (!line) return;
   121	    lines.push(line);
   122	    if (shouldShowLine(line) && line !== lastPrintedLine) {
   123	      console.log(line);
   124	      lastPrintedLine = line;
   125	      sawProgress = true;
   126	    }
   127	  }
   128	
   129	  function onChunk(chunk) {
   130	    pending += chunk.toString();
   131	    const parts = pending.split("\n");
   132	    pending = parts.pop();
   133	    parts.forEach(flushLine);
   134	  }
   135	
   136	  child.stdout.on("data", onChunk);
   137	  child.stderr.on("data", onChunk);
   138	
   139	  return new Promise((resolve) => {
   140	    child.on("error", (error) => {
   141	      if (settled) return;
   142	      settled = true;
   143	      if (pending) flushLine(pending);
   144	      const detail = error && error.code
   145	        ? `spawn failed: ${error.message} (${error.code})`
   146	        : `spawn failed: ${error.message}`;
   147	      lines.push(detail);
   148	      resolve({ status: 1, output: lines.join("\n"), sawProgress: false });
   149	    });
   150	
   151	    child.on("close", (code) => {
   152	      if (settled) return;
   153	      settled = true;
   154	      if (pending) flushLine(pending);
   155	      resolve({ status: code ?? 1, output: lines.join("\n"), sawProgress });
   156	    });
   157	  });
   158	}
   159	
   160	function step(n, total, msg) {
   161	  console.log("");
   162	  console.log(`  [${n}/${total}] ${msg}`);
   163	  console.log(`  ${"─".repeat(50)}`);
   164	}

   166	function getInstalledOpenshellVersion(versionOutput = null) {
   167	  const output = String(versionOutput ?? runCapture("openshell -V", { ignoreError: true })).trim();
   168	  const match = output.match(/openshell\s+([0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+)/i);
   169	  if (!match) return null;
   170	  return match[1];
   171	}

   179	function buildSandboxConfigSyncScript(selectionConfig) {
   180	  // openclaw.json is immutable (root:root 444, Landlock read-only) — never
   181	  // write to it at runtime.  Model routing is handled by the host-side
   182	  // gateway (`openshell inference set` in Step 5), not from inside the
   183	  // sandbox.  We only write the NemoClaw selection config (~/.nemoclaw/).
   184	  return `
   185	set -euo pipefail
   186	mkdir -p ~/.nemoclaw
   187	cat > ~/.nemoclaw/config.json <<'EOF_NEMOCLAW_CFG'
   188	${JSON.stringify(selectionConfig, null, 2)}
   189	EOF_NEMOCLAW_CFG
   190	exit
   191	`.trim();
   192	}

   253	function installOpenshell() {
   254	  const result = spawnSync("bash", [path.join(SCRIPTS, "install-openshell.sh")], {
   255	    cwd: ROOT,
   256	    env: process.env,
   257	    stdio: ["ignore", "pipe", "pipe"],
   258	    encoding: "utf-8",
   259	  });
   260	  if (result.status !== 0) {
   261	    const output = `${result.stdout || ""}${result.stderr || ""}`.trim();
   262	    if (output) {
   263	      console.error(output);
   264	    }
   265	    return false;
   266	  }
   267	  const localBin = process.env.XDG_BIN_HOME || path.join(process.env.HOME || "", ".local", "bin");
   268	  if (fs.existsSync(path.join(localBin, "openshell")) && !process.env.PATH.split(path.delimiter).includes(localBin)) {
   269	    process.env.PATH = `${localBin}${path.delimiter}${process.env.PATH}`;
   270	  }
   271	  return isOpenshellInstalled();
   272	}

   278	function waitForSandboxReady(sandboxName, attempts = 10, delaySeconds = 2) {
   279	  for (let i = 0; i < attempts; i += 1) {
   280	    const exists = runCapture(`openshell sandbox get "${sandboxName}" 2>/dev/null`, { ignoreError: true });
   281	    if (exists) return true;
   282	    sleep(delaySeconds);
   283	  }
   284	  return false;
   285	}

   294	function isSafeModelId(value) {
   295	  return /^[A-Za-z0-9._:/-]+$/.test(value);
   296	}

   298	function getNonInteractiveProvider() {
   299	  const providerKey = (process.env.NEMOCLAW_PROVIDER || "").trim().toLowerCase();
   300	  if (!providerKey) return null;
   301	
   302	  const validProviders = new Set(["cloud", "ollama", "vllm", "nim"]);
   303	  if (!validProviders.has(providerKey)) {
   304	    console.error(`  Unsupported NEMOCLAW_PROVIDER: ${providerKey}`);
   305	    console.error("  Valid values: cloud, ollama, vllm, nim");
   306	    process.exit(1);
   307	  }
   308	
   309	  return providerKey;
   310	}
   311	
   312	function getNonInteractiveModel(providerKey) {
   313	  const model = (process.env.NEMOCLAW_MODEL || "").trim();
   314	  if (!model) return null;
   315	  if (!isSafeModelId(model)) {
   316	    console.error(`  Invalid NEMOCLAW_MODEL for provider '${providerKey}': ${model}`);
   317	    console.error("  Model values may only contain letters, numbers, '.', '_', ':', '/', and '-'.");
   318	    process.exit(1);
   319	  }
   320	  return model;
   321	}

   323	// ── Step 1: Preflight ────────────────────────────────────────────
   324	
   325	async function preflight() {
   326	  step(1, 7, "Preflight checks");
   327	
   328	  // Docker
   329	  if (!isDockerRunning()) {
   330	    console.error("  Docker is not running. Please start Docker and try again.");
   331	    process.exit(1);
   332	  }
   333	  console.log("  ✓ Docker is running");
   334	
   335	  const runtime = getContainerRuntime();
   336	  if (isUnsupportedMacosRuntime(runtime)) {
   337	    console.error("  Podman on macOS is not supported by NemoClaw at this time.");
   338	    console.error("  OpenShell currently depends on Docker host-gateway behavior that Podman on macOS does not provide.");
   339	    console.error("  Use Colima or Docker Desktop on macOS instead.");
   340	    process.exit(1);
   341	  }
   342	  if (runtime !== "unknown") {
   343	    console.log(`  ✓ Container runtime: ${runtime}`);
   344	  }
   345	
   346	  // OpenShell CLI
   347	  if (!isOpenshellInstalled()) {
   348	    console.log("  openshell CLI not found. Installing...");
   349	    if (!installOpenshell()) {
   350	      console.error("  Failed to install openshell CLI.");
   351	      console.error("  Install manually: https://github.com/NVIDIA/OpenShell/releases");
   352	      process.exit(1);
   353	    }
   354	  }
   355	  console.log(`  ✓ openshell CLI: ${runCapture("openshell --version 2>/dev/null || echo unknown", { ignoreError: true })}`);
   356	
   357	  // Clean up stale NemoClaw session before checking ports.
   358	  // A previous onboard run may have left the gateway container and port
   359	  // forward running.  If a NemoClaw-owned gateway is still present, tear
   360	  // it down so the port check below doesn't fail on our own leftovers.
   361	  const gwInfo = runCapture("openshell gateway info -g nemoclaw 2>/dev/null", { ignoreError: true });
   362	  if (hasStaleGateway(gwInfo)) {
   363	    console.log("  Cleaning up previous NemoClaw session...");
   364	    run("openshell forward stop 18789 2>/dev/null || true", { ignoreError: true });
   365	    run("openshell gateway destroy -g nemoclaw 2>/dev/null || true", { ignoreError: true });
   366	    console.log("  ✓ Previous session cleaned up");
   367	  }
   368	
   369	  // Required ports — gateway (8080) and dashboard (18789)
   370	  const requiredPorts = [
   371	    { port: 8080, label: "OpenShell gateway" },
   372	    { port: 18789, label: "NemoClaw dashboard" },
   373	  ];
   374	  for (const { port, label } of requiredPorts) {
   375	    const portCheck = await checkPortAvailable(port);
   376	    if (!portCheck.ok) {
   377	      console.error("");
   378	      console.error(`  !! Port ${port} is not available.`);
   379	      console.error(`     ${label} needs this port.`);
   380	      console.error("");
   381	      if (portCheck.process && portCheck.process !== "unknown") {
   382	        console.error(`     Blocked by: ${portCheck.process}${portCheck.pid ? ` (PID ${portCheck.pid})` : ""}`);
   383	        console.error("");
   384	        console.error("     To fix, stop the conflicting process:");
   385	        console.error("");
   386	        if (portCheck.pid) {
   387	          console.error(`       sudo kill ${portCheck.pid}`);
   388	        } else {
   389	          console.error(`       lsof -i :${port} -sTCP:LISTEN -P -n`);
   390	        }
   391	        console.error("       # or, if it's a systemd service:");
   392	        console.error("       systemctl --user stop openclaw-gateway.service");
   393	      } else {
   394	        console.error(`     Could not identify the process using port ${port}.`);
   395	        console.error(`     Run: lsof -i :${port} -sTCP:LISTEN`);
   396	      }
   397	      console.error("");
   398	      console.error(`     Detail: ${portCheck.reason}`);
   399	      process.exit(1);
   400	    }
   401	    console.log(`  ✓ Port ${port} available (${label})`);
   402	  }
   403	
   404	  // GPU
   405	  const gpu = nim.detectGpu();
   406	  if (gpu && gpu.type === "nvidia") {
   407	    console.log(`  ✓ NVIDIA GPU detected: ${gpu.count} GPU(s), ${gpu.totalMemoryMB} MB VRAM`);
   408	  } else if (gpu && gpu.type === "apple") {
   409	    console.log(`  ✓ Apple GPU detected: ${gpu.name}${gpu.cores ? ` (${gpu.cores} cores)` : ""}, ${gpu.totalMemoryMB} MB unified memory`);
   410	    console.log("  ⓘ NIM requires NVIDIA GPU — will use cloud inference");
   411	  } else {
   412	    console.log("  ⓘ No GPU detected — will use cloud inference");
   413	  }
   414	
   415	  return gpu;
   416	}
   417	
   418	// ── Step 2: Gateway ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   419	
   420	async function startGateway(gpu) {
   421	  step(2, 7, "Starting OpenShell gateway");
   422	
   423	  // Destroy old gateway
   424	  run("openshell gateway destroy -g nemoclaw 2>/dev/null || true", { ignoreError: true });
   425	
   426	  const gwArgs = ["--name", "nemoclaw"];
   427	  // Do NOT pass --gpu here. On DGX Spark (and most GPU hosts), inference is
   428	  // routed through a host-side provider (Ollama, vLLM, or cloud API) — the
   429	  // sandbox itself does not need direct GPU access. Passing --gpu causes
   430	  // FailedPrecondition errors when the gateway's k3s device plugin cannot
   431	  // allocate GPUs. See: https://build.nvidia.com/spark/nemoclaw/instructions
   432	  const gatewayEnv = {};
   433	  const openshellVersion = getInstalledOpenshellVersion();
   434	  const stableGatewayImage = openshellVersion
   435	    ? `ghcr.io/nvidia/openshell/cluster:${openshellVersion}`
   436	    : null;
   437	  if (stableGatewayImage && openshellVersion) {
   438	    gatewayEnv.OPENSHELL_CLUSTER_IMAGE = stableGatewayImage;
   439	    gatewayEnv.IMAGE_TAG = openshellVersion;
   440	    console.log(`  Using pinned OpenShell gateway image: ${stableGatewayImage}`);
   441	  }
   442	
   443	  run(`openshell gateway start ${gwArgs.join(" ")}`, {
   444	    ignoreError: false,
   445	    env: gatewayEnv,
   446	  });
   447	
   448	  // Verify health
   449	  for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
   450	    const status = runCapture("openshell status 2>&1", { ignoreError: true });
   451	    if (status.includes("Connected")) {
   452	      console.log("  ✓ Gateway is healthy");
   453	      break;
   454	    }
   455	    if (i === 4) {
   456	      console.error("  Gateway failed to start. Run: openshell gateway info");
   457	      process.exit(1);
   458	    }
   459	    sleep(2);
   460	  }
   461	
   462	  // CoreDNS fix — always run. k3s-inside-Docker has broken DNS on all platforms.
   463	  const runtime = getContainerRuntime();
   464	  if (shouldPatchCoredns(runtime)) {
   465	    console.log("  Patching CoreDNS for Colima...");
   466	    run(`bash "${path.join(SCRIPTS, "fix-coredns.sh")}" nemoclaw 2>&1 || true`, { ignoreError: true });
   467	  }
   468	  // Give DNS a moment to propagate
   469	  sleep(5);
   470	}
   471

   622	async function setupNim(sandboxName, gpu) {
   623	  step(4, 7, "Configuring inference (NIM)");
   624	
   625	  let model = null;
   626	  let provider = "nvidia-nim";
   627	  let nimContainer = null;
   628	
   629	  // Detect local inference options
   630	  const hasOllama = !!runCapture("command -v ollama", { ignoreError: true });
   631	  const ollamaRunning = !!runCapture("curl -sf http://localhost:11434/api/tags 2>/dev/null", { ignoreError: true });
   632	  const vllmRunning = !!runCapture("curl -sf http://localhost:8000/v1/models 2>/dev/null", { ignoreError: true });
   633	  const requestedProvider = isNonInteractive() ? getNonInteractiveProvider() : null;
   634	  const requestedModel = isNonInteractive() ? getNonInteractiveModel(requestedProvider || "cloud") : null;
   635	  // Build options list — only show local options with NEMOCLAW_EXPERIMENTAL=1
   636	  const options = [];
   637	  if (EXPERIMENTAL && gpu && gpu.nimCapable) {
   638	    options.push({ key: "nim", label: "Local NIM container (NVIDIA GPU) [experimental]" });
   639	  }
   640	  options.push({
   641	    key: "cloud",
   642	    label:
   643	      "NVIDIA Endpoint API (build.nvidia.com)" +
   644	      (!ollamaRunning && !(EXPERIMENTAL && vllmRunning) ? " (recommended)" : ""),
   645	  });
   646	  if (hasOllama || ollamaRunning) {
   647	    options.push({
   648	      key: "ollama",
   649	      label:
   650	        `Local Ollama (localhost:11434)${ollamaRunning ? " — running" : ""}` +
   651	        (ollamaRunning ? " (suggested)" : ""),
   652	    });
   653	  }
   654	  if (EXPERIMENTAL && vllmRunning) {
   655	    options.push({
   656	      key: "vllm",
   657	      label: "Existing vLLM instance (localhost:8000) — running [experimental] (suggested)",
   658	    });
   659	  }
   660	
   661	  // On macOS without Ollama, offer to install it
   662	  if (!hasOllama && process.platform === "darwin") {
   663	    options.push({ key: "install-ollama", label: "Install Ollama (macOS)" });
   664	  }
   665	
   666	  if (options.length > 1) {
   667	    let selected;
   668	
   669	    if (isNonInteractive()) {
   670	      const providerKey = requestedProvider || "cloud";
   671	      selected = options.find((o) => o.key === providerKey);
   672	      if (!selected) {
   673	        console.error(`  Requested provider '${providerKey}' is not available in this environment.`);
   674	        process.exit(1);
   675	      }
   676	      note(`  [non-interactive] Provider: ${selected.key}`);
   677	    } else {
   678	      const suggestions = [];
   679	      if (vllmRunning) suggestions.push("vLLM");
   680	      if (ollamaRunning) suggestions.push("Ollama");
   681	      if (suggestions.length > 0) {
   682	        console.log(`  Detected local inference option${suggestions.length > 1 ? "s" : ""}: ${suggestions.join(", ")}`);
   683	        console.log("  Select one explicitly to use it. Press Enter to keep the cloud default.");
   684	        console.log("");
   685	      }
   686	
   687	      console.log("");
   688	      console.log("  Inference options:");
   689	      options.forEach((o, i) => {
   690	        console.log(`    ${i + 1}) ${o.label}`);
   691	      });
   692	      console.log("");
   693	
   694	      const defaultIdx = options.findIndex((o) => o.key === "cloud") + 1;
   695	      const choice = await prompt(`  Choose [${defaultIdx}]: `);
   696	      const idx = parseInt(choice || String(defaultIdx), 10) - 1;
   697	      selected = options[idx] || options[defaultIdx - 1];
   698	    }
   699	
   700	    if (selected.key === "nim") {
   701	      // List models that fit GPU VRAM
   702	      const models = nim.listModels().filter((m) => m.minGpuMemoryMB <= gpu.totalMemoryMB);
   703	      if (models.length === 0) {
   704	        console.log("  No NIM models fit your GPU VRAM. Falling back to cloud API.");
   705	      } else {
   706	        let sel;
   707	        if (isNonInteractive()) {
   708	          if (requestedModel) {
   709	            sel = models.find((m) => m.name === requestedModel);
   710	            if (!sel) {
   711	              console.error(`  Unsupported NEMOCLAW_MODEL for NIM: ${requestedModel}`);
   712	              process.exit(1);
   713	            }
   714	          } else {
   715	            sel = models[0];
   716	          }
   717	          note(`  [non-interactive] NIM model: ${sel.name}`);
   718	        } else {
   719	          console.log("");
   720	          console.log("  Models that fit your GPU:");
   721	          models.forEach((m, i) => {
   722	            console.log(`    ${i + 1}) ${m.name} (min ${m.minGpuMemoryMB} MB)`);
   723	          });
   724	          console.log("");
   725	
   726	          const modelChoice = await prompt(`  Choose model [1]: `);
   727	          const midx = parseInt(modelChoice || "1", 10) - 1;
   728	          sel = models[midx] || models[0];
   729	        }
   730	        model = sel.name;
   731	
   732	        console.log(`  Pulling NIM image for ${model}...`);
   733	        nim.pullNimImage(model);
   734	
   735	        console.log("  Starting NIM container...");
   736	        nimContainer = nim.startNimContainer(sandboxName, model);
   737	
   738	        console.log("  Waiting for NIM to become healthy...");
   739	        if (!nim.waitForNimHealth()) {
   740	          console.error("  NIM failed to start. Falling back to cloud API.");
   741	          model = null;
   742	          nimContainer = null;
   743	        } else {
   744	          provider = "vllm-local";
   745	        }
   746	      }
   747	    } else if (selected.key === "ollama") {
   748	      if (!ollamaRunning) {
   749	        console.log("  Starting Ollama...");
   750	        run("OLLAMA_HOST=0.0.0.0:11434 ollama serve > /dev/null 2>&1 &", { ignoreError: true });
   751	        sleep(2);
   752	      }
   753	      console.log("  ✓ Using Ollama on localhost:11434");
   754	      provider = "ollama-local";
   755	      if (isNonInteractive()) {
   756	        model = requestedModel || getDefaultOllamaModel(runCapture);
   757	      } else {
   758	        model = await promptOllamaModel();
   759	      }
   760	    } else if (selected.key === "install-ollama") {
   761	      console.log("  Installing Ollama via Homebrew...");
   762	      run("brew install ollama", { ignoreError: true });
   763	      console.log("  Starting Ollama...");
   764	      run("OLLAMA_HOST=0.0.0.0:11434 ollama serve > /dev/null 2>&1 &", { ignoreError: true });
   765	        sleep(2);
   766	      console.log("  ✓ Using Ollama on localhost:11434");
   767	      provider = "ollama-local";
   768	      if (isNonInteractive()) {
   769	        model = requestedModel || getDefaultOllamaModel(runCapture);
   770	      } else {
   771	        model = await promptOllamaModel();
   772	      }
   773	    } else if (selected.key === "vllm") {
   774	      console.log("  ✓ Using existing vLLM on localhost:8000");
   775	      provider = "vllm-local";
   776	      model = "vllm-local";
   777	    }
   778	    // else: cloud — fall through to default below
   779	  }
   780	
   781	  if (provider === "nvidia-nim") {
   782	    if (isNonInteractive()) {
   783	      // In non-interactive mode, NVIDIA_API_KEY must be set via env var
   784	      if (!process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY) {
   785	        console.error("  NVIDIA_API_KEY is required for cloud provider in non-interactive mode.");
   786	        console.error("  Set it via: NVIDIA_API_KEY=nvapi-... nemoclaw onboard --non-interactive");
   787	        process.exit(1);
   788	      }
   789	    } else {
   790	      await ensureApiKey();
   791	      model = model || (await promptCloudModel()) || DEFAULT_CLOUD_MODEL;
   792	    }
   793	    model = model || requestedModel || DEFAULT_CLOUD_MODEL;
   794	    console.log(`  Using NVIDIA Endpoint API with model: ${model}`);
   795	  }
   796	
   797	  registry.updateSandbox(sandboxName, { model, provider, nimContainer });
   798	
   799	  return { model, provider };
   800	}

   804	async function setupInference(sandboxName, model, provider) {
   805	  step(5, 7, "Setting up inference provider");
   806	
   807	  if (provider === "nvidia-nim") {
   808	    // Create nvidia-nim provider
   809	    run(
   810	      `openshell provider create --name nvidia-nim --type openai ` +
   811	      `--credential ${shellQuote("NVIDIA_API_KEY=" + process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY)} ` +
   812	      `--config "OPENAI_BASE_URL=https://integrate.api.nvidia.com/v1" 2>&1 || true`,
   813	      { ignoreError: true }
   814	    );
   815	    run(
   816	      `openshell inference set --no-verify --provider nvidia-nim --model ${shellQuote(model)} 2>/dev/null || true`,
   817	      { ignoreError: true }
   818	    );
   819	  } else if (provider === "vllm-local") {
   820	    const validation = validateLocalProvider(provider, runCapture);
   821	    if (!validation.ok) {
   822	      console.error(`  ${validation.message}`);
   823	      process.exit(1);
   824	    }
   825	    const baseUrl = getLocalProviderBaseUrl(provider);
   826	    run(
   827	      `openshell provider create --name vllm-local --type openai ` +
   828	      `--credential "OPENAI_API_KEY=dummy" ` +
   829	      `--config "OPENAI_BASE_URL=${baseUrl}" 2>&1 || ` +
   830	      `openshell provider update vllm-local --credential "OPENAI_API_KEY=dummy" ` +
   831	      `--config "OPENAI_BASE_URL=${baseUrl}" 2>&1 || true`,
   832	      { ignoreError: true }
   833	    );
   834	    run(
   835	      `openshell inference set --no-verify --provider vllm-local --model ${shellQuote(model)} 2>/dev/null || true`,
   836	      { ignoreError: true }
   837	    );
   838	  } else if (provider === "ollama-local") {
   839	    const validation = validateLocalProvider(provider, runCapture);
   840	    if (!validation.ok) {
   841	      console.error(`  ${validation.message}`);
   842	      console.error("  On macOS, local inference also depends on OpenShell host routing support.");
   843	      process.exit(1);
   844	    }
   845	    const baseUrl = getLocalProviderBaseUrl(provider);
   846	    run(
   847	      `openshell provider create --name ollama-local --type openai ` +
   848	      `--credential "OPENAI_API_KEY=ollama" ` +
   849	      `--config "OPENAI_BASE_URL=${baseUrl}" 2>&1 || ` +
   850	      `openshell provider update ollama-local --credential "OPENAI_API_KEY=ollama" ` +
   851	      `--config "OPENAI_BASE_URL=${baseUrl}" 2>&1 || true`,
   852	      { ignoreError: true }
   853	    );
   854	    run(
   855	      `openshell inference set --no-verify --provider ollama-local --model ${shellQuote(model)} 2>/dev/null || true`,
   856	      { ignoreError: true }
   857	    );
   858	    console.log(`  Priming Ollama model: ${model}`);
   859	    run(getOllamaWarmupCommand(model), { ignoreError: true });
   860	    const probe = validateOllamaModel(model, runCapture);

    16	function run(cmd, opts = {}) {
    17	  const stdio = opts.stdio ?? ["ignore", "inherit", "inherit"];
    18	  const result = spawnSync("bash", ["-c", cmd], {
    19	    ...opts,
    20	    stdio,
    21	    cwd: ROOT,
    22	    env: { ...process.env, ...opts.env },
    23	  });
    24	  if (result.status !== 0 && !opts.ignoreError) {
    25	    console.error(`  Command failed (exit ${result.status}): ${cmd.slice(0, 80)}`);
    26	    process.exit(result.status || 1);
    27	  }
    28	  return result;
    29	}
    30	
    31	function runInteractive(cmd, opts = {}) {
    32	  const stdio = opts.stdio ?? "inherit";
    33	  const result = spawnSync("bash", ["-c", cmd], {
    34	    ...opts,
    35	    stdio,
    36	    cwd: ROOT,
    37	    env: { ...process.env, ...opts.env },
    38	  });
    39	  if (result.status !== 0 && !opts.ignoreError) {
    40	    console.error(`  Command failed (exit ${result.status}): ${cmd.slice(0, 80)}`);
    41	    process.exit(result.status || 1);
    42	  }
    43	  return result;
    44	}
    45	
    46	function runCapture(cmd, opts = {}) {
    47	  try {
    48	    return execSync(cmd, {
    49	      ...opts,
    50	      encoding: "utf-8",
    51	      cwd: ROOT,
    52	      env: { ...process.env, ...opts.env },
    53	      stdio: ["pipe", "pipe", "pipe"],
    54	    }).trim();
    55	  } catch (err) {
    56	    if (opts.ignoreError) return "";
    57	    throw err;
    58	  }
    59	}
    60	
    61	/**
    62	 * Shell-quote a value for safe interpolation into bash -c strings.
    63	 * Wraps in single quotes and escapes embedded single quotes.
    64	 */
    65	function shellQuote(value) {
    66	  return `'${String(value).replace(/'/g, `'\\''`)}'`;
    67	}
    68	
    69	/**
    70	 * Validate a name (sandbox, instance, container) against RFC 1123 label rules.
    71	 * Rejects shell metacharacters, path traversal, and empty/overlength names.
    72	 */
    73	function validateName(name, label = "name") {
    74	  if (!name || typeof name !== "string") {
    75	    throw new Error(`${label} is required`);
    76	  }
    77	  if (name.length > 63) {
    78	    throw new Error(`${label} too long (max 63 chars): '${name.slice(0, 20)}...'`);
    79	  }
    80	  if (!/^[a-z0-9]([a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?$/.test(name)) {
    81	    throw new Error(
    82	      `Invalid ${label}: '${name}'. Must be lowercase alphanumeric with optional internal hyphens.`
    83	    );
    84	  }
    85	  return name;
    86	}

     9	const CREDS_DIR = path.join(process.env.HOME || "/tmp", ".nemoclaw");
    10	const CREDS_FILE = path.join(CREDS_DIR, "credentials.json");
    11	
    12	function loadCredentials() {
    13	  try {
    14	    if (fs.existsSync(CREDS_FILE)) {
    15	      return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(CREDS_FILE, "utf-8"));
    16	    }
    17	  } catch {}
    18	  return {};
    19	}
    20	
    21	function saveCredential(key, value) {
    22	  fs.mkdirSync(CREDS_DIR, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });
    23	  const creds = loadCredentials();
    24	  creds[key] = value;
    25	  fs.writeFileSync(CREDS_FILE, JSON.stringify(creds, null, 2), { mode: 0o600 });
    26	}
    27	
    28	function getCredential(key) {
    29	  if (process.env[key]) return process.env[key];
    30	  const creds = loadCredentials();
    31	  return creds[key] || null;
    32	}
    33	
    34	function prompt(question) {
    35	  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    36	    const rl = readline.createInterface({ input: process.stdin, output: process.stderr });
    37	    rl.question(question, (answer) => {
    38	      rl.close();
    39	      if (!process.stdin.isTTY) {
    40	        if (typeof process.stdin.pause === "function") {
    41	          process.stdin.pause();
    42	        }
    43	        if (typeof process.stdin.unref === "function") {
    44	          process.stdin.unref();
    45	        }
    46	      }
    47	      resolve(answer.trim());
    48	    });
    49	  });
    50	}
    51

Now let me understand the full picture. The issue is that:

1. In `onboard.js` line 811, the NVIDIA API key is passed as a command-line argument to `openshell provider create`:
```
`--credential ${shellQuote("NVIDIA_API_KEY=" + process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY)} `
```

2. In `onboard.js` lines 537-538, the NVIDIA API key is passed as an environment variable argument to `openshell sandbox create`:
```
envArgs.push(`NVIDIA_API_KEY=${shellQuote(process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY)}`);
```
This gets passed in the shell command:
```
`openshell sandbox create ${createArgs.join(" ")} -- env ${envArgs.join(" ")} nemoclaw-start 2>&1`
```

Both of these expose the API key in `ps aux`.

The PR description suggests three approaches:
1. Pass the credential via stdin
2. Pass via environment variable
3. Pass via a temporary file with restricted permissions

Let me look at how `openshell provider create` works and whether it supports stdin or environment variables for credentials. Let me search for the openshell CLI usage:

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	# SPDX-FileCopyrightText: Copyright (c) 2026 NVIDIA CORPORATION & AFFILIATES. All rights reserved.
     3	# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     4	#
     5	# NemoClaw setup — run this on the HOST to set up everything.
     6	#
     7	# Prerequisites:
     8	#   - Docker running (Colima, Docker Desktop, or native)
     9	#   - openshell CLI installed (pip install openshell @ git+https://github.com/NVIDIA/OpenShell.git)
    10	#   - NVIDIA_API_KEY set in environment (from build.nvidia.com)
    11	#
    12	# Usage:
    13	#   export NVIDIA_API_KEY=nvapi-...
    14	#   ./scripts/setup.sh [sandbox-name]
    15	#
    16	# What it does:
    17	#   1. Starts an OpenShell gateway (or reuses existing)
    18	#   2. Fixes CoreDNS for Colima environments
    19	#   3. Creates nvidia-nim provider (build.nvidia.com)
    20	#   4. Creates vllm-local provider (if vLLM is running)
    21	#   5. Sets inference route to nvidia-nim by default
    22	#   6. Builds and creates the NemoClaw sandbox
    23	#   7. Prints next steps
    24	
    25	set -euo pipefail
    26	
    27	RED='\033[0;31m'
    28	GREEN='\033[0;32m'
    29	YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
    30	NC='\033[0m'
    31	
    32	SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"
    33	REPO_DIR="$(cd "$SCRIPT_DIR/.." && pwd)"
    34	# shellcheck source=./lib/runtime.sh
    35	. "$SCRIPT_DIR/lib/runtime.sh"
    36	
    37	info() { echo -e "${GREEN}>>>${NC} $1"; }
    38	warn() { echo -e "${YELLOW}>>>${NC} $1"; }
    39	fail() { echo -e "${RED}>>>${NC} $1"; exit 1; }
    40	
    41	upsert_provider() {
    42	  local name="$1"
    43	  local type="$2"
    44	  local credential="$3"
    45	  local config="$4"
    46	
    47	  if openshell provider create --name "$name" --type "$type" \
    48	    --credential "$credential" \
    49	    --config "$config" 2>&1 | grep -q "AlreadyExists"; then
    50	    openshell provider update "$name" \
    51	      --credential "$credential" \
    52	      --config "$config" > /dev/null
    53	    info "Updated $name provider"
    54	  else
    55	    info "Created $name provider"
    56	  fi
    57	}
    58	
    59	# Resolve DOCKER_HOST for macOS user-scoped runtimes when needed.
    60	ORIGINAL_DOCKER_HOST="${DOCKER_HOST:-}"
    61	if docker_host="$(detect_docker_host)"; then
    62	  export DOCKER_HOST="$docker_host"
    63	  if [ -n "$ORIGINAL_DOCKER_HOST" ]; then
    64	    warn "Using DOCKER_HOST from environment: $docker_host"
    65	  else
    66	    case "$(docker_host_runtime "$docker_host" || true)" in
    67	      colima)
    68	        warn "Using Colima Docker socket: ${docker_host#unix://}"
    69	        ;;
    70	      docker-desktop)
    71	        warn "Using Docker Desktop socket: ${docker_host#unix://}"
    72	        ;;
    73	      custom)
    74	        warn "Using Docker host: $docker_host"
    75	        ;;
    76	    esac
    77	  fi
    78	fi
    79	
    80	# Check prerequisites
    81	command -v openshell > /dev/null || fail "openshell CLI not found. Install the binary from https://github.com/NVIDIA/OpenShell/releases"
    82	command -v docker > /dev/null || fail "docker not found"
    83	[ -n "${NVIDIA_API_KEY:-}" ] || fail "NVIDIA_API_KEY not set. Get one from build.nvidia.com"
    84	
    85	CONTAINER_RUNTIME="$(infer_container_runtime_from_info "$(docker info 2>/dev/null || true)")"
    86	if is_unsupported_macos_runtime "$(uname -s)" "$CONTAINER_RUNTIME"; then
    87	  fail "Podman on macOS is not supported yet. NemoClaw currently depends on OpenShell support for Podman on macOS. Use Colima or Docker Desktop instead."
    88	fi
    89	if [ "$CONTAINER_RUNTIME" != "unknown" ]; then
    90	  info "Container runtime: $CONTAINER_RUNTIME"
    91	fi
    92	SANDBOX_NAME="${1:-nemoclaw}"
    93	info "Using sandbox name: ${SANDBOX_NAME}"
    94	
    95	OPEN_SHELL_VERSION_RAW="$(openshell -V 2>/dev/null || true)"
    96	OPEN_SHELL_VERSION_LOWER="${OPEN_SHELL_VERSION_RAW,,}"
    97	if [[ "$OPEN_SHELL_VERSION_LOWER" =~ openshell[[:space:]]+([0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+) ]]; then
    98	  export IMAGE_TAG="${BASH_REMATCH[1]}"
    99	  export OPENSHELL_CLUSTER_IMAGE="ghcr.io/nvidia/openshell/cluster:${BASH_REMATCH[1]}"
   100	  info "Using pinned OpenShell gateway image: ${OPENSHELL_CLUSTER_IMAGE}"
   101	elif [[ -n "$OPEN_SHELL_VERSION_RAW" ]]; then
   102	  warn "Could not parse openshell version from 'openshell -V': ${OPEN_SHELL_VERSION_RAW}"
   103	  warn "Skipping OpenShell gateway image pinning."
   104	fi
   105	
   106	# 1. Gateway — always start fresh to avoid stale state
   107	info "Starting OpenShell gateway..."
   108	openshell gateway destroy -g nemoclaw > /dev/null 2>&1 || true
   109	GATEWAY_ARGS=(--name nemoclaw)
   110	command -v nvidia-smi > /dev/null 2>&1 && GATEWAY_ARGS+=(--gpu)
   111	openshell gateway start "${GATEWAY_ARGS[@]}" 2>&1 | grep -E "Gateway|✓|Error|error" || true
   112	
   113	# Verify gateway is actually healthy (may need a moment after start)
   114	for i in 1 2 3 4 5; do
   115	  if openshell status 2>&1 | grep -q "Connected"; then
   116	    break
   117	  fi
   118	  [ "$i" -eq 5 ] && fail "Gateway failed to start. Check 'openshell gateway info' and Docker logs."
   119	  sleep 2
   120	done
   121	info "Gateway is healthy"
   122	
   123	# 2. CoreDNS fix (Colima only)
   124	if [ "$CONTAINER_RUNTIME" = "colima" ]; then
   125	  info "Patching CoreDNS for Colima..."
   126	  bash "$SCRIPT_DIR/fix-coredns.sh" nemoclaw 2>&1 || warn "CoreDNS patch failed (may not be needed)"
   127	fi
   128	
   129	# 3. Providers
   130	info "Setting up inference providers..."
   131	
   132	# nvidia-nim (build.nvidia.com)
   133	upsert_provider \
   134	  "nvidia-nim" \
   135	  "openai" \
   136	  "NVIDIA_API_KEY=$NVIDIA_API_KEY" \
   137	  "OPENAI_BASE_URL=https://integrate.api.nvidia.com/v1"
   138	
   139	# vllm-local (if vLLM is installed or running)
   140	if check_local_provider_health "vllm-local" || python3 -c "import vllm" 2>/dev/null; then
   141	  VLLM_LOCAL_BASE_URL="$(get_local_provider_base_url "vllm-local")"
   142	  upsert_provider \
   143	    "vllm-local" \
   144	    "openai" \
   145	    "OPENAI_API_KEY=dummy" \
   146	    "OPENAI_BASE_URL=$VLLM_LOCAL_BASE_URL"
   147	fi
   148	
   149	# 4a. Ollama (macOS local inference)
   150	if [ "$(uname -s)" = "Darwin" ]; then
   151	  if ! command -v ollama > /dev/null 2>&1; then
   152	    info "Installing Ollama..."
   153	    brew install ollama 2>/dev/null || warn "Ollama install failed (brew required). Install manually: https://ollama.com"
   154	  fi
   155	  if command -v ollama > /dev/null 2>&1; then
   156	    # Start Ollama service if not running
   157	    if ! check_local_provider_health "ollama-local"; then
   158	      info "Starting Ollama service..."
   159	      OLLAMA_HOST=0.0.0.0:11434 ollama serve > /dev/null 2>&1 &
   160	      sleep 2
   161	    fi
   162	    OLLAMA_LOCAL_BASE_URL="$(get_local_provider_base_url "ollama-local")"
   163	    upsert_provider \
   164	      "ollama-local" \
   165	      "openai" \
   166	      "OPENAI_API_KEY=ollama" \
   167	      "OPENAI_BASE_URL=$OLLAMA_LOCAL_BASE_URL"
   168	  fi
   169	fi
   170	
   171	# 4b. Inference route — default to nvidia-nim
   172	info "Setting inference route to nvidia-nim / Nemotron 3 Super..."
   173	openshell inference set --no-verify --provider nvidia-nim --model nvidia/nemotron-3-super-120b-a12b > /dev/null 2>&1
   174	
   175	# 5. Build and create sandbox
   176	info "Deleting old ${SANDBOX_NAME} sandbox (if any)..."
   177	openshell sandbox delete "$SANDBOX_NAME" > /dev/null 2>&1 || true
   178	
   179	info "Building and creating NemoClaw sandbox (this takes a few minutes on first run)..."
   180	
   181	# Stage a clean build context (openshell doesn't honor .dockerignore)
   182	BUILD_CTX="$(mktemp -d)"
   183	cp "$REPO_DIR/Dockerfile" "$BUILD_CTX/"
   184	cp -r "$REPO_DIR/nemoclaw" "$BUILD_CTX/nemoclaw"
   185	cp -r "$REPO_DIR/nemoclaw-blueprint" "$BUILD_CTX/nemoclaw-blueprint"
   186	cp -r "$REPO_DIR/scripts" "$BUILD_CTX/scripts"
   187	rm -rf "$BUILD_CTX/nemoclaw/node_modules"
   188	
   189	# Capture full output to a temp file so we can filter for display but still
   190	# detect failures. The raw log is kept on failure for debugging.
   191	CREATE_LOG=$(mktemp /tmp/nemoclaw-create-XXXXXX.log)
   192	set +e
   193	openshell sandbox create --from "$BUILD_CTX/Dockerfile" --name "$SANDBOX_NAME" \
   194	  --provider nvidia-nim \
   195	  -- env NVIDIA_API_KEY="$NVIDIA_API_KEY" > "$CREATE_LOG" 2>&1
   196	CREATE_RC=$?
   197	set -e
   198	rm -rf "$BUILD_CTX"
   199	
   200	# Show progress lines (filter apt noise and env var dumps that contain NVIDIA_API_KEY)
   201	grep -E "^  (Step |Building |Built |Pushing |\[progress\]|Successfully |Created sandbox|Image )|✓" "$CREATE_LOG" || true
   202	
   203	if [ "$CREATE_RC" != "0" ]; then
   204	  echo ""
   205	  warn "Last 20 lines of build output:"
   206	  tail -20 "$CREATE_LOG" | grep -v "NVIDIA_API_KEY"
   207	  echo ""
   208	  fail "Sandbox creation failed (exit $CREATE_RC). Full log: $CREATE_LOG"
   209	fi
   210	rm -f "$CREATE_LOG"
   211	
   212	# Verify sandbox is Ready (not just that a record exists)
   213	# Strip ANSI color codes before checking phase
   214	SANDBOX_LINE=$(openshell sandbox list 2>&1 | sed 's/\x1b\[[0-9;]*m//g' | awk -v name="$SANDBOX_NAME" '$1 == name { print; exit }')
   215	if ! echo "$SANDBOX_LINE" | grep -q "Ready"; then
   216	  SANDBOX_PHASE=$(echo "$SANDBOX_LINE" | awk '{print $NF}')
   217	  echo ""
   218	  warn "Sandbox phase: ${SANDBOX_PHASE:-unknown}"
   219	  # Check for common failure modes
   220	  SB_DETAIL=$(openshell sandbox get "$SANDBOX_NAME" 2>&1 || true)
   221	  if echo "$SB_DETAIL" | grep -qi "ImagePull\|ErrImagePull\|image.*not found"; then
   222	    warn "Image pull failure detected. The sandbox image was built inside the"
   223	    warn "gateway but k3s can't find it. This is a known openshell issue."
   224	    warn "Workaround: run 'openshell gateway destroy && openshell gateway start'"
   225	    warn "and re-run this script."
   226	  fi
   227	  fail "Sandbox created but not Ready (phase: ${SANDBOX_PHASE:-unknown}). Check 'openshell sandbox get ${SANDBOX_NAME}'."
   228	fi
   229	
   230	# 6. Done
   231	echo ""
   232	info "Setup complete!"
   233	echo ""
   234	echo "  openclaw agent --agent main --local -m 'how many rs are there in strawberry?' --session-id s1"
   235	echo ""
   236

   145	ensure_clean_start() {
   146	  if [ "$ALLOW_EXISTING_STATE" = true ]; then
   147	    return 0
   148	  fi

   152	  fi
   153

   155	    if openshell sandbox list 2>/dev/null | grep -Eq '[[:alnum:]]'; then
   156	      fail "Existing OpenShell sandboxes detected. Re-run with --allow-existing-state only if you are prepared for uninstall.sh to remove them."
   157	    fi
   158	  fi
   159	}

   161	feed_install_answers() {
   162	  local answers_pipe="$1"
   163	  local install_log="$2"
   164	
   165	  (
   166	    printf '%s\n' "$SANDBOX_NAME"
   167	
   168	    while :; do
   169	      if [ -f "$install_log" ] && grep -q "OpenClaw gateway launched inside sandbox" "$install_log"; then
   170	        break
   171	      fi
   172	      sleep 1
   173	    done
   174	
   175	    printf 'n\n'
   176	  ) > "$answers_pipe"
   177	}

   179	start_log_follow() {
   180	  local logfile="$1"
   181	  : > "$logfile"
   182	  tail -n +1 -f "$logfile" &
   183	  LOG_FOLLOW_PID=$!
   184	}
   185	
   186	stop_log_follow() {
   187	  if [ -n "$LOG_FOLLOW_PID" ] && kill -0 "$LOG_FOLLOW_PID" 2>/dev/null; then
   188	    kill "$LOG_FOLLOW_PID" 2>/dev/null || true
   189	    wait "$LOG_FOLLOW_PID" 2>/dev/null || true
   190	  fi
   191	  LOG_FOLLOW_PID=""
   192	}
   193	
   194	run_install() {
   195	  local answers_pipe="$1"
   196	  info "Running install.sh with sandbox '$SANDBOX_NAME'"
   197	  feed_install_answers "$answers_pipe" "$INSTALL_LOG" &
   198	  ANSWER_WRITER_PID=$!
   199	  start_log_follow "$INSTALL_LOG"
   200	  set +e
   201	  bash "$REPO_DIR/install.sh" < "$answers_pipe" >> "$INSTALL_LOG" 2>&1
   202	  INSTALL_STATUS=$?
   203	  set -e
   204	  stop_log_follow
   205	  stop_answer_writer
   206	  return 0
   207	}
   208	
   209	run_uninstall() {
   210	  local -a args=(--yes)
   211	  if [ "$KEEP_OPEN_SHELL" = true ]; then
   212	    args+=(--keep-openshell)
   213	  fi
   214	  if [ "$DELETE_MODELS" = true ]; then
   215	    args+=(--delete-models)
   216	  fi
   217	
   218	  info "Running uninstall.sh for cleanup"
   219	  start_log_follow "$UNINSTALL_LOG"
   220	  set +e
   221	  bash "$REPO_DIR/uninstall.sh" "${args[@]}" >> "$UNINSTALL_LOG" 2>&1
   222	  UNINSTALL_STATUS=$?
   223	  set -e
   224	  stop_log_follow
   225	  return 0
   226	}
   227	
   228	verify_cleanup() {
   229	  local leftovers=0
   230	
   231	  if [ -d "$HOME/.nemoclaw" ] || [ -d "$HOME/.config/nemoclaw" ]; then
   232	    warn "NemoClaw state directories still exist under HOME."
   233	    leftovers=1
   234	  fi
   235	
   236	  if command -v openshell > /dev/null 2>&1; then
   237	    local sandbox_output
   238	    sandbox_output="$(openshell sandbox list 2>/dev/null || true)"
   239	    if printf '%s' "$sandbox_output" | grep -Eq '[[:alnum:]]'; then
   240	      warn "OpenShell still reports sandbox entries after uninstall."
   241	      leftovers=1
   242	    fi
   243	  fi
   244	
   245	  if command -v docker > /dev/null 2>&1 && docker info > /dev/null 2>&1; then
   246	    local related_containers
   247	    related_containers="$(
   248	      docker ps -a --format '{{.Image}} {{.Names}}' 2>/dev/null \
   249	        | awk 'BEGIN { IGNORECASE=1 } /openshell-cluster|openshell|openclaw|nemoclaw/ { print }'
   250	    )"
   251	    if [ -n "$related_containers" ]; then
   252	      warn "Related Docker containers remain after uninstall:"
   253	      printf '%s\n' "$related_containers"
   254	      leftovers=1
   255	    fi
   256	  fi
   257	
   258	  return "$leftovers"
   259	}
   260	
   261	cleanup() {
   262	  stop_log_follow
   263	
   264	  stop_answer_writer
   265	
   266	  if [ -n "$ANSWERS_PIPE" ] && [ -p "$ANSWERS_PIPE" ]; then
   267	    rm -f "$ANSWERS_PIPE"
   268	  fi
   269	
   270	  if [ -n "$UNINSTALL_LOG" ]; then
   271	    run_uninstall
   272	    if [ "$UNINSTALL_STATUS" -ne 0 ]; then
   273	      warn "uninstall.sh exited with status $UNINSTALL_STATUS"
   274	    fi
   275	    if ! verify_cleanup; then
   276	      warn "Cleanup verification found leftover state."
   277	    else
   278	      info "Cleanup verification passed"
   279	    fi
   280	  fi
   281	
   282	  if [ "$KEEP_LOGS" = false ] && [ "$INSTALL_STATUS" -eq 0 ] && [ "$UNINSTALL_STATUS" -eq 0 ]; then
   283	    rm -f "$INSTALL_LOG" "$UNINSTALL_LOG"
   284	    rmdir "$LOG_DIR" 2>/dev/null || true
   285	  else
   286	    info "Install log: $INSTALL_LOG"
   287	    info "Uninstall log: $UNINSTALL_LOG"
   288	  fi
   289	}
   290	
   291	main() {
   292	  validate_sandbox_name
   293	  select_runtime
   294	  ensure_clean_start
   295	
   296	  mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
   297	  local stamp
   298	  stamp="$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)"
   299	  INSTALL_LOG="$LOG_DIR/install-$stamp.log"
   300	  UNINSTALL_LOG="$LOG_DIR/uninstall-$stamp.log"
   301	
   302	  ANSWERS_PIPE="$(mktemp -u "${TMPDIR:-/tmp}/nemoclaw-smoke-answers-XXXXXX")"
   303	  mkfifo "$ANSWERS_PIPE"
   304	  trap cleanup EXIT
   305	
   306	  info "Logs will be written under $LOG_DIR"
   307	  run_install "$ANSWERS_PIPE"
   308	
   309	  if [ "$INSTALL_STATUS" -ne 0 ]; then
   310	    fail "install.sh failed with status $INSTALL_STATUS. See $INSTALL_LOG"
   311	  fi
   312	
   313	  info "install.sh completed successfully"
   314	}
   315	
   316	if [ "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}" = "$0" ]; then
   317	  main "$@"
   318	fi

    52	resolve_default_sandbox_name() {

   101	  info "=== Installation complete ==="
   102	  printf "\n"
   103	  printf "  ${C_GREEN}${C_BOLD}NemoClaw${C_RESET}  ${C_DIM}(%ss)${C_RESET}\n" "$elapsed"
   104	  printf "\n"
   105	  printf "  ${C_GREEN}Your OpenClaw Sandbox is live.${C_RESET}\n"
   106	  printf "  ${C_DIM}Sandbox in, break things, and tell us what you find.${C_RESET}\n"
   107	  printf "\n"
   108	  printf "  ${C_GREEN}Next:${C_RESET}\n"
   109	  printf "  %s$%s nemoclaw %s connect\n" "$C_GREEN" "$C_RESET" "$sandbox_name"
   110	  printf "  %ssandbox@%s$%s openclaw tui\n" "$C_GREEN" "$sandbox_name" "$C_RESET"
   111	  printf "\n"
   112	  printf "  ${C_BOLD}GitHub${C_RESET}  ${C_DIM}https://github.com/nvidia/nemoclaw${C_RESET}\n"
   113	  printf "  ${C_BOLD}Docs${C_RESET}    ${C_DIM}https://docs.nvidia.com/nemoclaw/latest/${C_RESET}\n"
   114	  printf "\n"
   115	}

   144	# spin "label" cmd [args...]
   145	#   Runs a command in the background, showing a braille spinner until it exits.
   146	#   Stdout/stderr are captured; dumped only on failure.
   147	#   Falls back to plain output when stdout is not a TTY (CI / piped installs).
   148	spin() {
   149	  local msg="$1"; shift
   150	
   151	  if [[ ! -t 1 ]]; then
   152	    info "$msg"
   153	    "$@"
   154	    return
   155	  fi
   156	
   157	  local log; log=$(mktemp)
   158	  "$@" >"$log" 2>&1 &
   159	  local pid=$! i=0
   160	  local frames=('⠋' '⠙' '⠹' '⠸' '⠼' '⠴' '⠦' '⠧' '⠇' '⠏')
   161	
   162	  while kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; do
   163	    printf "\r  ${C_GREEN}%s${C_RESET}  %s" "${frames[$((i++ % 10))]}" "$msg"
   164	    sleep 0.08
   165	  done
   166	
   167	  if wait "$pid"; then
   168	    local status=0
   169	  else
   170	    local status=$?
   171	  fi
   172	  if [[ $status -eq 0 ]]; then
   173	    printf "\r  ${C_GREEN}✓${C_RESET}  %s\n" "$msg"
   174	  else
   175	    printf "\r  ${C_RED}✗${C_RESET}  %s\n\n" "$msg"
   176	    cat "$log" >&2
   177	    printf "\n"
   178	  fi
   179	  rm -f "$log"
   180	  return $status
   181	}
   182	
   183	command_exists() { command -v "$1" &>/dev/null; }
   184	
   185	MIN_NODE_MAJOR=20
   186	MIN_NPM_MAJOR=10
   187	RECOMMENDED_NODE_MAJOR=22
   188	RUNTIME_REQUIREMENT_MSG="NemoClaw requires Node.js >=${MIN_NODE_MAJOR} and npm >=${MIN_NPM_MAJOR} (recommended Node.js ${RECOMMENDED_NODE_MAJOR})."
   189	NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR="${HOME}/.local/bin"
   190	ORIGINAL_PATH="${PATH:-}"
   191	
   192	# Compare two semver strings (major.minor.patch). Returns 0 if $1 >= $2.
   193	version_gte() {
   194	  local IFS=.
   195	  local -a a=($1) b=($2)
   196	  for i in 0 1 2; do
   197	    local ai=${a[$i]:-0} bi=${b[$i]:-0}
   198	    if (( ai > bi )); then return 0; fi
   199	    if (( ai < bi )); then return 1; fi
   200	  done
   201	  return 0
   202	}
   203	
   204	# Ensure nvm environment is loaded in the current shell.
   205	ensure_nvm_loaded() {
   206	  if [[ -z "${NVM_DIR:-}" ]]; then
   207	    export NVM_DIR="$HOME/.nvm"
   208	  fi
   209	  if [[ -s "$NVM_DIR/nvm.sh" ]]; then
   210	    \. "$NVM_DIR/nvm.sh"
   211	  fi
   212	}
   213	
   214	# Refresh PATH so that npm global bin is discoverable.
   215	# After nvm installs Node.js the global bin lives under the nvm prefix,
   216	# which may not yet be on PATH in the current session.
   217	refresh_path() {
   218	  ensure_nvm_loaded
   219	
   220	  local npm_bin
   221	  npm_bin="$(npm config get prefix 2>/dev/null)/bin" || true
   222	  if [[ -n "$npm_bin" && -d "$npm_bin" && ":$PATH:" != *":$npm_bin:"* ]]; then
   223	    export PATH="$npm_bin:$PATH"
   224	  fi
   225	
   226	  if [[ -d "$NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR" && ":$PATH:" != *":$NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR:"* ]]; then
   227	    export PATH="$NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR:$PATH"
   228	  fi
   229	}
   230	
   231	ensure_nemoclaw_shim() {
   232	  local npm_bin shim_path
   233	  npm_bin="$(npm config get prefix 2>/dev/null)/bin" || true
   234	  shim_path="${NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR}/nemoclaw"
   235	
   236	  if [[ -z "$npm_bin" || ! -x "$npm_bin/nemoclaw" ]]; then
   237	    return 1
   238	  fi
   239	
   240	  if [[ ":$ORIGINAL_PATH:" == *":$npm_bin:"* ]] || [[ ":$ORIGINAL_PATH:" == *":$NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR:"* ]]; then
   241	    return 0
   242	  fi
   243	
   244	  mkdir -p "$NEMOCLAW_SHIM_DIR"
   245	  ln -sfn "$npm_bin/nemoclaw" "$shim_path"
   246	  refresh_path
   247	  info "Created user-local shim at $shim_path"
   248	  return 0
   249	}
   250	
   251	version_major() {
   252	  printf '%s\n' "${1#v}" | cut -d. -f1
   253	}
   254	
   255	ensure_supported_runtime() {
   256	  command_exists node || error "${RUNTIME_REQUIREMENT_MSG} Node.js was not found on PATH."
   257	  command_exists npm || error "${RUNTIME_REQUIREMENT_MSG} npm was not found on PATH."
   258	
   259	  local node_version npm_version node_major npm_major
   260	  node_version="$(node --version 2>/dev/null || true)"
   261	  npm_version="$(npm --version 2>/dev/null || true)"
   262	  node_major="$(version_major "$node_version")"
   263	  npm_major="$(version_major "$npm_version")"
   264	
   265	  [[ "$node_major" =~ ^[0-9]+$ ]] || error "Could not determine Node.js version from '${node_version}'. ${RUNTIME_REQUIREMENT_MSG}"
   266	  [[ "$npm_major" =~ ^[0-9]+$ ]] || error "Could not determine npm version from '${npm_version}'. ${RUNTIME_REQUIREMENT_MSG}"
   267	
   268	  if (( node_major < MIN_NODE_MAJOR || npm_major < MIN_NPM_MAJOR )); then
   269	    error "Unsupported runtime detected: Node.js ${node_version:-unknown}, npm ${npm_version:-unknown}. ${RUNTIME_REQUIREMENT_MSG} Upgrade Node.js and rerun the installer."
   270	  fi
   271	
   272	  info "Runtime OK: Node.js ${node_version}, npm ${npm_version}"
   273	}
   274	
   275	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   276	# 1. Node.js
   277	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   278	install_nodejs() {
   279	  if command_exists node; then
   280	    info "Node.js found: $(node --version)"
   281	    return
   282	  fi
   283	
   284	  info "Node.js not found — installing via nvm…"
   285	  # IMPORTANT: update NVM_SHA256 when changing NVM_VERSION
   286	  local NVM_VERSION="v0.40.4"
   287	  local NVM_SHA256="4b7412c49960c7d31e8df72da90c1fb5b8cccb419ac99537b737028d497aba4f"
   288	  local nvm_tmp
   289	  nvm_tmp="$(mktemp)"
   290	  curl -fsSL "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nvm-sh/nvm/${NVM_VERSION}/install.sh" -o "$nvm_tmp" \
   291	    || { rm -f "$nvm_tmp"; error "Failed to download nvm installer"; }
   292	  local actual_hash
   293	  if command_exists sha256sum; then
   294	    actual_hash="$(sha256sum "$nvm_tmp" | awk '{print $1}')"
   295	  elif command_exists shasum; then
   296	    actual_hash="$(shasum -a 256 "$nvm_tmp" | awk '{print $1}')"
   297	  else
   298	    warn "No SHA-256 tool found — skipping nvm integrity check"
   299	    actual_hash="$NVM_SHA256"  # allow execution
   300	  fi
   301	  if [[ "$actual_hash" != "$NVM_SHA256" ]]; then
   302	    rm -f "$nvm_tmp"
   303	    error "nvm installer integrity check failed\n  Expected: $NVM_SHA256\n  Actual:   $actual_hash"
   304	  fi
   305	  info "nvm installer integrity verified"
   306	  spin "Installing nvm..." bash "$nvm_tmp"
   307	  rm -f "$nvm_tmp"
   308	  ensure_nvm_loaded
   309	  spin "Installing Node.js ${RECOMMENDED_NODE_MAJOR}..." bash -c ". \"$NVM_DIR/nvm.sh\" && nvm install ${RECOMMENDED_NODE_MAJOR} --no-progress"
   310	  ensure_nvm_loaded
   311	  nvm use "${RECOMMENDED_NODE_MAJOR}" --silent
   312	  info "Node.js installed: $(node --version)"
   313	}
   314	
   315	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   316	# 2. Ollama
   317	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   318	OLLAMA_MIN_VERSION="0.18.0"
   319	
   320	get_ollama_version() {
   321	  # `ollama --version` outputs something like "ollama version 0.18.0"
   322	  ollama --version 2>/dev/null | grep -oE '[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+' | head -1
   323	}
   324	
   325	detect_gpu() {
   326	  # Returns 0 if a GPU is detected
   327	  if command_exists nvidia-smi; then
   328	    nvidia-smi &>/dev/null && return 0
   329	  fi
   330	  return 1
   331	}
   332	
   333	get_vram_mb() {
   334	  # Returns total VRAM in MiB (NVIDIA only). Falls back to 0.
   335	  if command_exists nvidia-smi; then
   336	    nvidia-smi --query-gpu=memory.total --format=csv,noheader,nounits 2>/dev/null \
   337	      | awk '{s += $1} END {print s+0}'
   338	    return
   339	  fi
   340	  # macOS — report unified memory as VRAM
   341	  if [[ "$(uname -s)" == "Darwin" ]] && command_exists sysctl; then
   342	    local bytes
   343	    bytes=$(sysctl -n hw.memsize 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
   344	    echo $(( bytes / 1024 / 1024 ))
   345	    return
   346	  fi
   347	  echo 0
   348	}
   349	
   350	install_or_upgrade_ollama() {
   351	  if detect_gpu && command_exists ollama; then
   352	    local current
   353	    current=$(get_ollama_version)
   354	    if [[ -n "$current" ]] && version_gte "$current" "$OLLAMA_MIN_VERSION"; then
   355	      info "Ollama v${current} meets minimum requirement (>= v${OLLAMA_MIN_VERSION})"
   356	    else
   357	      info "Ollama v${current:-unknown} is below v${OLLAMA_MIN_VERSION} — upgrading…"
   358	      curl -fsSL https://ollama.com/install.sh | sh
   359	      info "Ollama upgraded to $(get_ollama_version)"
   360	    fi
   361	  else
   362	    # No ollama — only install if a GPU is present
   363	    if detect_gpu; then
   364	      info "GPU detected — installing Ollama…"
   365	      curl -fsSL https://ollama.com/install.sh | sh
   366	      info "Ollama installed: v$(get_ollama_version)"
   367	    else
   368	      warn "No GPU detected — skipping Ollama installation."
   369	      return
   370	    fi
   371	  fi
   372	
   373	  # Pull the appropriate model based on VRAM
   374	  local vram_mb
   375	  vram_mb=$(get_vram_mb)
   376	  local vram_gb=$(( vram_mb / 1024 ))
   377	  info "Detected ${vram_gb} GB VRAM"
   378	
   379	  if (( vram_gb >= 120 )); then
   380	    info "Pulling nemotron-3-super:120b…"
   381	    ollama pull nemotron-3-super:120b
   382	  else
   383	    info "Pulling nemotron-3-nano:30b…"
   384	    ollama pull nemotron-3-nano:30b
   385	  fi
   386	}
   387	
   388	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   389	# 3. NemoClaw
   390	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   391	# Work around openclaw tarball missing directory entries (GH-503).
   392	# npm's tar extractor hard-fails because the tarball is missing directory
   393	# entries for extensions/, skills/, and dist/plugin-sdk/config/. System tar
   394	# handles this fine. We pre-extract openclaw into node_modules BEFORE npm
   395	# install so npm sees the dependency is already satisfied and skips it.
   396	pre_extract_openclaw() {
   397	  local install_dir="$1"
   398	  local openclaw_version
   399	  openclaw_version=$(node -e "console.log(require('${install_dir}/package.json').dependencies.openclaw)" 2>/dev/null || echo "")
   400	
   401	  if [[ -z "$openclaw_version" ]]; then
   402	    warn "Could not determine openclaw version — skipping pre-extraction"
   403	    return 1
   404	  fi
   405	
   406	  info "Pre-extracting openclaw@${openclaw_version} with system tar (GH-503 workaround)…"
   407	  local tmpdir
   408	  tmpdir="$(mktemp -d)"
   409	  if npm pack "openclaw@${openclaw_version}" --pack-destination "$tmpdir" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
   410	    local tgz
   411	    tgz="$(find "$tmpdir" -maxdepth 1 -name 'openclaw-*.tgz' -print -quit)"
   412	    if [[ -n "$tgz" && -f "$tgz" ]]; then
   413	      if mkdir -p "${install_dir}/node_modules/openclaw" \
   414	        && tar xzf "$tgz" -C "${install_dir}/node_modules/openclaw" --strip-components=1
   415	      then
   416	        info "openclaw pre-extracted successfully"
   417	      else
   418	        warn "Failed to extract openclaw tarball"
   419	        rm -rf "$tmpdir"
   420	        return 1
   421	      fi
   422	    else
   423	      warn "npm pack succeeded but tarball not found"
   424	      rm -rf "$tmpdir"
   425	      return 1
   426	    fi
   427	  else
   428	    warn "Failed to download openclaw tarball"
   429	    rm -rf "$tmpdir"
   430	    return 1
   431	  fi
   432	  rm -rf "$tmpdir"
   433	}

Now let me look more carefully at how the `openshell provider create` works. The key insight from the PR description is:

> Pass the credential via stdin, environment variable, or a temporary file with restricted permissions — not as a command-line argument.

The `run` function already passes `process.env` to the child process. So if `openshell provider create` reads the credential from an environment variable named after the provider's credential env (e.g., `NVIDIA_API_KEY`), we could avoid passing it on the command line.

But looking at the current code, the credential is passed as `--credential "NVIDIA_API_KEY=xxx"`. The `openshell` CLI likely stores this credential and uses it when making API calls. It probably doesn't read `NVIDIA_API_KEY` from the environment directly.

Let me check if there's a way to pass the credential via stdin. The `run` function uses `spawnSync` with `bash -c`. We could use stdin redirection.

Actually, let me re-examine the structure. The `streamSandboxCreate` function already uses `spawn` with stdio options. And `run` uses `spawnSync`. 

For the `openshell provider create` command, we need to avoid having the API key in the process list. The best approaches:

1. Pass the credential via stdin (if `openshell provider create` supports it)
2. Use a temporary file with restricted permissions
3. Pass via environment variable that the CLI reads

Since we don't know exactly what the `openshell` CLI supports, let me look at whether there's any reference to `--credential` being read from stdin or a file.

   103	async function deploy(instanceName) {
   104	  if (!instanceName) {
   105	    console.error("  Usage: nemoclaw deploy <instance-name>");
   106	    console.error("");
   107	    console.error("  Examples:");
   108	    console.error("    nemoclaw deploy my-gpu-box");
   109	    console.error("    nemoclaw deploy nemoclaw-prod");
   110	    console.error("    nemoclaw deploy nemoclaw-test");
   111	    process.exit(1);
   112	  }
   113	  await ensureApiKey();
   114	  if (isRepoPrivate("NVIDIA/OpenShell")) {
   115	    await ensureGithubToken();
   116	  }
   117	  validateName(instanceName, "instance name");
   118	  const name = instanceName;
   119	  const qname = shellQuote(name);
   120	  const gpu = process.env.NEMOCLAW_GPU || "a2-highgpu-1g:nvidia-tesla-a100:1";
   121	
   122	  console.log("");
   123	  console.log(`  Deploying NemoClaw to Brev instance: ${name}`);
   124	  console.log("");
   125	
   126	  try {
   127	    execFileSync("which", ["brev"], { stdio: "ignore" });
   128	  } catch {
   129	    console.error("brev CLI not found. Install: https://brev.nvidia.com");
   130	    process.exit(1);
   131	  }
   132	
   133	  let exists = false;
   134	  try {
   135	    const out = execFileSync("brev", ["ls"], { encoding: "utf-8" });
   136	    exists = out.includes(name);
   137	  } catch (err) {
   138	    if (err.stdout && err.stdout.includes(name)) exists = true;
   139	    if (err.stderr && err.stderr.includes(name)) exists = true;
   140	  }
   141	
   142	  if (!exists) {
   143	    console.log(`  Creating Brev instance '${name}' (${gpu})...`);
   144	    run(`brev create ${qname} --gpu ${shellQuote(gpu)}`);
   145	  } else {
   146	    console.log(`  Brev instance '${name}' already exists.`);
   147	  }
   148	
   149	  run(`brev refresh`, { ignoreError: true });
   150	
   151	  process.stdout.write(`  Waiting for SSH `);
   152	  for (let i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
   153	    try {
   154	      execFileSync("ssh", ["-o", "ConnectTimeout=5", "-o", "StrictHostKeyChecking=no", name, "echo", "ok"], { encoding: "utf-8", stdio: "ignore" });
   155	      process.stdout.write(` ${G}✓${R}\n`);
   156	      break;
   157	    } catch {
   158	      if (i === 59) {
   159	        process.stdout.write("\n");
   160	        console.error(`  Timed out waiting for SSH to ${name}`);
   161	        process.exit(1);
   162	      }
   163	      process.stdout.write(".");
   164	      spawnSync("sleep", ["3"]);
   165	    }
   166	  }
   167	
   168	  console.log("  Syncing NemoClaw to VM...");
   169	  run(`ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o LogLevel=ERROR ${qname} 'mkdir -p /home/ubuntu/nemoclaw'`);
   170	  run(`rsync -az --delete --exclude node_modules --exclude .git --exclude src -e "ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o LogLevel=ERROR" "${ROOT}/scripts" "${ROOT}/Dockerfile" "${ROOT}/nemoclaw" "${ROOT}/nemoclaw-blueprint" "${ROOT}/bin" "${ROOT}/package.json" ${qname}:/home/ubuntu/nemoclaw/`);

   182	  const envTmp = path.join(envDir, "env");
   183	  fs.writeFileSync(envTmp, envLines.join("\n") + "\n", { mode: 0o600 });
   184	  try {
   185	    run(`scp -q -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o LogLevel=ERROR ${shellQuote(envTmp)} ${qname}:/home/ubuntu/nemoclaw/.env`);
   186	  } finally {
   187	    try { fs.unlinkSync(envTmp); } catch {}
   188	    try { fs.rmdirSync(envDir); } catch {}
   189	  }
   190	
   191	  console.log("  Running setup...");
   192	  runInteractive(`ssh -t -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o LogLevel=ERROR ${qname} 'cd /home/ubuntu/nemoclaw && set -a && . .env && set +a && bash scripts/brev-setup.sh'`);
   193

   195	    console.log("  Starting services...");
   196	    run(`ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o LogLevel=ERROR ${qname} 'cd /home/ubuntu/nemoclaw && set -a && . .env && set +a && bash scripts/start-services.sh'`);

   199	  console.log("");

   201	  console.log("");
   202	  runInteractive(`ssh -t -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o LogLevel=ERROR ${qname} 'cd /home/ubuntu/nemoclaw && set -a && . .env && set +a && openshell sandbox connect nemoclaw'`);
   203	}

   205	async function start() {
   206	  await ensureApiKey();
   207	  const { defaultSandbox } = registry.listSandboxes();
   208	  const safeName = defaultSandbox && /^[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$/.test(defaultSandbox) ? defaultSandbox : null;
   209	  const sandboxEnv = safeName ? `SANDBOX_NAME=${shellQuote(safeName)}` : "";
   210	  run(`${sandboxEnv} bash "${SCRIPTS}/start-services.sh"`);
   211	}
   212	
   213	function stop() {
   214	  run(`bash "${SCRIPTS}/start-services.sh" --stop`);
   215	}

   217	function debug(args) {
   218	  const result = spawnSync("bash", [path.join(SCRIPTS, "debug.sh"), ...args], {
   219	    stdio: "inherit",
   220	    cwd: ROOT,
   221	    env: {
   222	      ...process.env,
   223	      SANDBOX_NAME: registry.listSandboxes().defaultSandbox || "",
   224	    },
   225	  });
   226	  exitWithSpawnResult(result);
   227	}
   228	
   229	function uninstall(args) {
   230	  const localScript = resolveUninstallScript();
   231	  if (localScript) {
   232	    console.log(`  Running local uninstall script: ${localScript}`);
   233	    const result = spawnSync("bash", [localScript, ...args], {
   234	      stdio: "inherit",
   235	      cwd: ROOT,
   236	      env: process.env,
   237	    });
   238	    exitWithSpawnResult(result);
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  console.log(`  Local uninstall script not found; falling back to ${REMOTE_UNINSTALL_URL}`);
   242	  const forwardedArgs = args.map(shellQuote).join(" ");
   243	  const command = forwardedArgs.length > 0
   244	    ? `curl -fsSL ${shellQuote(REMOTE_UNINSTALL_URL)} | bash -s -- ${forwardedArgs}`
   245	    : `curl -fsSL ${shellQuote(REMOTE_UNINSTALL_URL)} | bash`;
   246	  const result = spawnSync("bash", ["-c", command], {
   247	    stdio: "inherit",
   248	    cwd: ROOT,
   249	    env: process.env,
   250	  });
   251	  exitWithSpawnResult(result);
   252	}

   254	function showStatus() {
   255	  // Show sandbox registry
   256	  const { sandboxes, defaultSandbox } = registry.listSandboxes();
   257	  if (sandboxes.length > 0) {
   258	    console.log("");
   259	    console.log("  Sandboxes:");
   260	    for (const sb of sandboxes) {
   261	      const def = sb.name === defaultSandbox ? " *" : "";
   262	      const model = sb.model ? ` (${sb.model})` : "";
   263	      console.log(`    ${sb.name}${def}${model}`);
   264	    }
   265	    console.log("");
   266	  }
   267	
   268	  // Show service status
   269	  run(`bash "${SCRIPTS}/start-services.sh" --status`);
   270	}
   271	
   272	function listSandboxes() {
   273	  const { sandboxes, defaultSandbox } = registry.listSandboxes();
   274	  if (sandboxes.length === 0) {
   275	    console.log("");
   276	    console.log("  No sandboxes registered. Run `nemoclaw onboard` to get started.");
   277	    console.log("");
   278	    return;
   279	  }
   280	
   281	  console.log("");
   282	  console.log("  Sandboxes:");
   283	  for (const sb of sandboxes) {
   284	    const def = sb.name === defaultSandbox ? " *" : "";
   285	    const model = sb.model || "unknown";
   286	    const provider = sb.provider || "unknown";
   287	    const gpu = sb.gpuEnabled ? "GPU" : "CPU";
   288	    const presets = sb.policies && sb.policies.length > 0 ? sb.policies.join(", ") : "none";
   289	    console.log(`    ${sb.name}${def}`);
   290	    console.log(`      model: ${model}  provider: ${provider}  ${gpu}  policies: ${presets}`);
   291	  }
   292	  console.log("");
   293	  console.log("  * = default sandbox");
   294	  console.log("");
   295	}

   299	function sandboxConnect(sandboxName) {
   300	  const qn = shellQuote(sandboxName);
   301	  // Ensure port forward is alive before connecting
   302	  run(`openshell forward start --background 18789 ${qn} 2>/dev/null || true`, { ignoreError: true });
   303	  runInteractive(`openshell sandbox connect ${qn}`);
   304	}

   306	function sandboxStatus(sandboxName) {
   307	  const sb = registry.getSandbox(sandboxName);
   308	  if (sb) {
   309	    console.log("");
   310	    console.log(`  Sandbox: ${sb.name}`);
   311	    console.log(`    Model:    ${sb.model || "unknown"}`);
   312	    console.log(`    Provider: ${sb.provider || "unknown"}`);
   313	    console.log(`    GPU:      ${sb.gpuEnabled ? "yes" : "no"}`);
   314	    console.log(`    Policies: ${(sb.policies || []).join(", ") || "none"}`);
   315	  }
   316	
   317	  // openshell info
   318	  run(`openshell sandbox get ${shellQuote(sandboxName)} 2>/dev/null || true`, { ignoreError: true });
   319	
   320	  // NIM health
   321	  const nimStat = nim.nimStatus(sandboxName);
   322	  console.log(`    NIM:      ${nimStat.running ? `running (${nimStat.container})` : "not running"}`);
   323	  if (nimStat.running) {
   324	    console.log(`    Healthy:  ${nimStat.healthy ? "yes" : "no"}`);
   325	  }
   326	  console.log("");
   327	}

   334	async function sandboxPolicyAdd(sandboxName) {
   335	  const allPresets = policies.listPresets();
   336	  const applied = policies.getAppliedPresets(sandboxName);
   337	
   338	  console.log("");
   339	  console.log("  Available presets:");
   340	  allPresets.forEach((p) => {
   341	    const marker = applied.includes(p.name) ? "●" : "○";
   342	    console.log(`    ${marker} ${p.name} — ${p.description}`);
   343	  });
   344	  console.log("");
   345	
   346	  const { prompt: askPrompt } = require("./lib/credentials");
   347	  const answer = await askPrompt("  Preset to apply: ");
   348	  if (!answer) return;
   349	
   350	  const confirm = await askPrompt(`  Apply '${answer}' to sandbox '${sandboxName}'? [Y/n]: `);
   351	  if (confirm.toLowerCase() === "n") return;
   352	
   353	  policies.applyPreset(sandboxName, answer);
   354	}
   355	
   356	function sandboxPolicyList(sandboxName) {
   357	  const allPresets = policies.listPresets();
   358	  const applied = policies.getAppliedPresets(sandboxName);
   359	
   360	  console.log("");
   361	  console.log(`  Policy presets for sandbox '${sandboxName}':`);
   362	  allPresets.forEach((p) => {
   363	    const marker = applied.includes(p.name) ? "●" : "○";
   364	    console.log(`    ${marker} ${p.name} — ${p.description}`);
   365	  });
   366	  console.log("");
   367	}

   369	async function sandboxDestroy(sandboxName, args = []) {
   370	  const skipConfirm = args.includes("--yes") || args.includes("--force");
   371	  if (!skipConfirm) {
   372	    const { prompt: askPrompt } = require("./lib/credentials");
   373	    const answer = await askPrompt(
   374	      `  ${YW}Destroy sandbox '${sandboxName}'?${R} This cannot be undone. [y/N]: `,
   375	    );
   376	    if (answer.trim().toLowerCase() !== "y" && answer.trim().toLowerCase() !== "yes") {
   377	      console.log("  Cancelled.");
   378	      return;
   379	    }
   380	  }
   381	
   382	  console.log(`  Stopping NIM for '${sandboxName}'...`);
   383	  nim.stopNimContainer(sandboxName);
   384	
   385	  console.log(`  Deleting sandbox '${sandboxName}'...`);
   386	  run(`openshell sandbox delete ${shellQuote(sandboxName)} 2>/dev/null || true`, { ignoreError: true });
   387	
   388	  registry.removeSandbox(sandboxName);
   389	  console.log(`  ${G}✓${R} Sandbox '${sandboxName}' destroyed`);
   390	}

Now I understand the codebase better. Let me focus on the specific changes needed.

The key issue is in:
1. `bin/lib/onboard.js` - lines 810-812 (and similar lines for other providers) where `--credential` includes the API key directly
2. `bin/lib/onboard.js` - lines 537-538 where `NVIDIA_API_KEY` is passed in env args for sandbox create  
3. `scripts/setup.sh` - lines 136-137 where `NVIDIA_API_KEY` is passed on command line
4. `bin/nemoclaw.js` - line 100 where `NVIDIA_API_KEY` is passed on command line for setup-spark

The approach should be to:
1. Use environment variables to pass credentials to child processes instead of command-line arguments
2. Use temporary files with restricted permissions for passing credentials to `openshell provider create`

Let me first create a script to verify the problem:







🎬 ACTION

const { run, shellQuote } = require("./bin/lib/runner");

// Simulate what onboard.js does currently
const fakeKey = "nvapi-test-key-12345";
process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY = fakeKey;

// This is what the current code does - the key would be visible in ps aux
const cmd = `echo "Provider create command would be: openshell provider create --name nvidia-nim --type openai --credential ${shellQuote("NVIDIA_API_KEY=" + process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY)}"`;
console.log("Current (vulnerable) approach:");
console.log("Command that would be run:");
console.log(cmd);
console.log("");

// The key is directly in the command string - visible to ps aux
if (cmd.includes(fakeKey)) {
  console.log("❌ PROBLEM: API key is visible in the command string!");
  console.log("   Any user running 'ps aux' would see: " + fakeKey);
} else {
  console.log("✓ API key is not in the command string");
}

> - #191 — use provider-specific credential environment variable

```js
function run(cmd, opts = {}) {
  const stdio = opts.stdio ?? ["ignore", "inherit", "inherit"];
  const result = spawnSync("bash", ["-c", cmd], {
    ...opts,
    stdio,
    cwd: ROOT,
    env: { ...process.env, ...opts.env },
  });
```

1. Move the credential into `opts.env` 
2. Use a temporary file to pass the credential to `openshell provider create`

This means instead of building a shell command string and passing it to `bash -c`, we should use `spawnSync`/`spawn` with direct argument arrays. Let me think about the right approach.\n\nThe issue is that API keys are passed as command-line arguments. The solution should be:\n\n1. For `openshell provider create --credential`, we should pass the credential via an environment variable rather than on the command line. The `openshell` CLI likely supports reading credentials from the environment. Looking at how `--credential` is formatted (`NVIDIA_API_KEY=xxx`), it seems like it\'s setting an environment variable for the provider. So maybe `openshell provider create` will read `NVIDIA_API_KEY` from its environment if `--credential` is not specified?\n\nBut wait, I don\'t know if that\'s how `openshell` works. Let me look at this from a different angle.\n\nThe PR description says:\n> - #148 — replace shell string interpolation with argv arrays\n> - #191 — use provider-specific credential environment variable\n\nThis suggests two changes:\n1. Instead of building a shell command string, use `spawnSync`/`spawn` with argument arrays (which avoids the shell interpolation issue)\n2. Use provider-specific credential environment variables\n\nFor change #1, instead of:\n```js\nrun(`openshell provider create --name nvidia-nim --type openai --credential ${shellQuote("NVIDIA_API_KEY=" + process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY)} ...`);\n```\n\nWe should use:\n```js\nspawnSync("openshell", ["provider", "create", "--name", "nvidia-nim", "--type", "openai", "--credential", `NVIDIA_API_KEY=${process.env.NVIDIA_API_KEY}`, ...], { env: ... });\n```\n\nBut this still exposes the key as an argument to `openshell` in `ps aux`.\n\nFor change #2, maybe `openshell provider create` can read the credential from an environment variable. For example, if we set `NVIDIA_API_KEY` in the process environment, `openshell provider create` might pick it up automatically.\n\nLet me look at the current code more carefully. 1. **Replace shell string interpolation with argv arrays**: Instead of building a full command string and passing it to `bash -c`, use `spawnSync`/`spawn` with argument arrays. This way, the arguments are passed directly to the process via `execve`, which doesn't expose them in the same way through `bash`.

But wait, even with argv arrays, the arguments are still visible in `/proc/[pid]/cmdline` and `ps aux`. So this alone doesn't solve the problem.

2. **Use provider-specific credential environment variable**: This is the real solution. Instead of passing the credential as a command-line argument (`--credential "NVIDIA_API_KEY=xxx"`), pass it as an environment variable. The `openshell` CLI should read the credential from the environment variable specified by the provider configuration.

Looking at `inference-config.js`:
```js
const DEFAULT_ROUTE_CREDENTIAL_ENV = "OPENAI_API_KEY";
```

This is the credential environment variable name used for routing. But for the `nvidia-nim` provider, the credential key is `NVIDIA_API_KEY`.

I think the solution is:
- For `openshell provider create`, we can pass the credential via an environment variable instead of `--credential`. The `openshell` CLI should be modified to read from `NVIDIA_API_KEY` env var when creating the nvidia-nim provider.

But we're not modifying `openshell` - we're modifying `nemoclaw`. So maybe the change is:
- Instead of passing the key on the command line, write it to a temporary file with restricted permissions and use `--credential-file` or pipe it via stdin.

Let me check if `openshell provider create` might support stdin:

   474	async function createSandbox(gpu) {
   475	  step(3, 7, "Creating sandbox");
   476	
   477	  const nameAnswer = await promptOrDefault(
   478	    "  Sandbox name (lowercase, numbers, hyphens) [my-assistant]: ",
   479	    "NEMOCLAW_SANDBOX_NAME", "my-assistant"
   480	  );
   481	  const sandboxName = (nameAnswer || "my-assistant").trim().toLowerCase();
   482	
   483	  // Validate: RFC 1123 subdomain — lowercase alphanumeric and hyphens,
   484	  // must start and end with alphanumeric (required by Kubernetes/OpenShell)
   485	  if (!/^[a-z0-9]([a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?$/.test(sandboxName)) {
   486	    console.error(`  Invalid sandbox name: '${sandboxName}'`);
   487	    console.error("  Names must be lowercase, contain only letters, numbers, and hyphens,");
   488	    console.error("  and must start and end with a letter or number.");
   489	    process.exit(1);
   490	  }
   491	
   492	  // Check if sandbox already exists in registry
   493	  const existing = registry.getSandbox(sandboxName);
   494	  if (existing) {
   495	    if (isNonInteractive()) {
   496	      if (process.env.NEMOCLAW_RECREATE_SANDBOX !== "1") {
   497	        console.error(`  Sandbox '${sandboxName}' already exists.`);
   498	        console.error("  Set NEMOCLAW_RECREATE_SANDBOX=1 to recreate it in non-interactive mode.");
   499	        process.exit(1);
   500	      }
   501	      note(`  [non-interactive] Sandbox '${sandboxName}' exists — recreating`);
   502	    } else {
   503	      const recreate = await prompt(`  Sandbox '${sandboxName}' already exists. Recreate? [y/N]: `);
   504	      if (recreate.toLowerCase() !== "y") {
   505	        console.log("  Keeping existing sandbox.");
   506	        return sandboxName;
   507	      }
   508	    }
   509	    // Destroy old sandbox
   510	    run(`openshell sandbox delete "${sandboxName}" 2>/dev/null || true`, { ignoreError: true });
   511	    registry.removeSandbox(sandboxName);

   513

   518	  fs.copyFileSync(path.join(ROOT, "Dockerfile"), path.join(buildCtx, "Dockerfile"));
   519	  run(`cp -r "${path.join(ROOT, "nemoclaw")}" "${buildCtx}/nemoclaw"`);
